stretchy="false">(</mo><munderover><mo>âˆ‘</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>âˆ’</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></munderover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{aligned}
C_k &amp;= \sum\limits_{i=0}^{n-1}y_k(\omega_n^{-k})^i\\
&amp;=\sum\limits_{i=0}^{n-1}(\sum\limits_{j=0}^{n-1}a_j(\omega_n^i)^j)(\omega_n^{-k})^i\\
&amp;=\sum\limits_{i=0}^{n-1}(\sum\limits_{j=0}^{n-1}a_j(\omega_n^{j-k})^i)\\
&amp;=\sum\limits_{j=0}^{n-1}a_j(\sum\limits_{i=0}^{n-1}(w_n^{j-k})^i)
\end{aligned}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut"
